## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / nonlinear oscillators
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The acceleration in such systems typically arises from restoring forces (functions of x) and damping forces (functions of v), possibly with nonlinear terms like cubic restoring forces (Duffing oscillator) or nonlinear damping (van der Pol oscillator).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force proportional to displacement)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring force plus linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring force with linear damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (nonlinear damping depending on position)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinear restoring force)
- Softening/hardening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x * abs(x) (asymmetric nonlinear restoring force approximation)
- Forced oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (harmonic external driving force)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) (time-modulated restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * abs(v) (quadratic velocity-dependent damping)
- Coulomb + viscous damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sign(v) (combined friction model)
- General polynomial restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (polynomial potential expansion)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 * v + c2 * v (mixed nonlinear coupling terms)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) → symmetric potential wells preserving oscillator symmetry
- Even-power restoring terms (x**2) → asymmetric potential indicating broken symmetry in the oscillator
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v → energy dissipation or injection (damping/driving)
- Terms like (1 - x**2)*v → amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-sustained oscillations (limit cycles)
- Cubic position term x**3 with same/opposite sign as linear term → hardening/softening spring behavior
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) → external periodic forcing or parametric excitation
- Absence of explicit time dependence → autonomous system; presence indicates non-autonomous forcing
- Quadratic velocity damping v*abs(v) → aerodynamic or turbulent drag regime
- Products x*v or x**2*v → nonlinear energy exchange between kinetic and potential modes
- Sign(v) terms → dry friction / Coulomb friction modeling with velocity-independent magnitude

### Candidate 4: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*v**3 + c4*v**2 + c5*log(c6*Abs(v) + 1)`
Set c3=0, c4=0, c6=1. Matches GT.
Candidate 4 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 5: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*Abs(v) + c4*log(c5*Abs(v) + 1)`
Set c3=0, c5=1. Matches GT.
Candidate 5 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 6: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v**c3 + c4*v + c5*log(c6*Abs(v) + 1) + v`
The `+ v` is explicit. Set c2=0, c6=1. Remaining: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c4*v + v + c5*log(Abs(v) + 1)` = `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + (c4+1)*v + c5*log(Abs(v) + 1)`. Matches GT.
Candidate 6 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 7: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*v**2 + c4*exp(c5*v)*log(c6*Abs(v) + 1)`
Need `c4*exp(c5*v)*log(c6*Abs(v)+1)` to equal `c*log(Abs(v)+1)`. This requires c5=0, making exp=1. Then c4*log(c6*Abs(v)+1). Set c3=0, c6=1. Matches GT.
Candidate 7 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 8: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*v**2 + c4*log(c5*Abs(v) + 1)`
Set c3=0, c5=1. Matches GT.
Candidate 8 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 9: `c0 + c1*x**3 + c2*sin(t) + c3*v + c4*Abs(v) + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*v) + 1)`
Need `c5*log(c6*exp(c7*v)+1)` to equal `c*log(Abs(v)+1)`. These are fundamentally different functions. log(c6*exp(c7*v)+1) is a softplus-type function, not log(Abs(v)+1). Cannot match.
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 10: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*exp(c4*v)*log(c5*Abs(v) + 1)`
Set c4=0, c5=1. Then c3*log(Abs(v)+1). Matches GT.
Candidate 10 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 11: `c0 + c1*x**3 + c2*sin(t) + c3*sin(c4*v + c5) + c6*v + c7*Abs(v)`
Has sin(c4*v+c5) instead of log(Abs(v)+1). sin is periodic, log is not. Cannot match. Even setting c3=0 leaves only v and Abs(v) terms, which are piecewise linear, not log.
Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 12: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*log(c4*Abs(v) + 1)`
With c4=1, this is exactly `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*log(Abs(v)+1)`. Matches GT perfectly.
Candidate 12 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 13: `c0 + c1*x**3 + c2*sin(t) + c3*v + c4*exp(c5*v) + c6*Abs(v) + c7*v*x`
Set c0=0, c4=0, c6=0, c7=0. Missing log(Abs(v)+1). Only has v term for v-dependence. Cannot match.
Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14: `c0 + c1*x**3 + c2*sin(t) + c3*v + c4*exp(c5*v) + c6*Abs(v)`

Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 15: `c0*x**3 + c1*sin(t) + c2*v + c3*v**2 + c4*v**3 + c5*Abs(v)`
Polynomial in v plus Abs(v). Cannot produce log(Abs(v)+1). 
Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 16: `(c0*v + (c1*v + c2)*(c3*x**3 + c4*sin(t) + c5*v + c6*Abs(v)))/(c1*v + c2)`
